namespace = SoAtEtE

# The Grand Master demands one of your sons due to debt
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1000
	hide_window = yes

	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = neognostic
			religion = sedevacantist
			religion = nestorian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		has_character_modifier = borrowed_from_knights_of_columbus
		NOT = { has_character_flag = sent_son_to_knights_of_columbus }
		any_child = {
			is_female = no
			is_adult = yes
			is_ruler = no
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { 
					current_heir = { 
						character = PREVPREV 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				is_adult = yes
				is_ruler = no
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { 
						current_heir = { 
							character = PREVPREV 
						}
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1001
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1001
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1002
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1002
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1003
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1003
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1003
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DEMAND_SON_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1003 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		set_character_flag = sent_son_to_knights_of_columbus
		
		piety = 100
		
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				FROMFROM = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						clear_wealth = PREV
					}
					spouse = {
						remove_spouse = spouse
						hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = SoAtE.2862 } }
					}
					move_character = PREV
					add_trait = celibate
					end_inaccessibility_effect = yes #removes in_hiding or in_seclusion

				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1003 # Pay them back
		wealth = -300
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_knights_of_columbus
		}
		FROM = {
			wealth = 300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_SOA_1003 # Refuse
		piety = -1000
	}
}

# Ping event when borrowing money from the Templars
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1010
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = -300
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1011
			}
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# Notification event when borrowing money from the Templars
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1011
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1011
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BORROW_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master demands the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1020
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = neognostic
			religion = sedevacantist
			religion = nestorian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		has_character_modifier = borrowed_from_knights_of_columbus
		NOT = { has_character_flag = sent_son_to_knights_of_columbus }
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 60
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1021
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1021
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1022
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1022
	
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1023
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1023
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1023
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_knights_of_columbus
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.1024 }
			}
		}
		
		piety = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1003 # Pay them back
		wealth = -300
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_knights_of_columbus
		}
		FROM = {
			wealth = 300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_SOA_1003 # Refuse
		piety = -1000
	}
}

# Castle has been erected
province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1024
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1024
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Knights of Columbus
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1030
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = neognostic
			religion = sedevacantist
			religion = nestorian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_knights_of_columbus
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = catholic
				religion = neognostic
				religion = sedevacantist
				religion = nestorian
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
				
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus
			}
		}
		
		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3.0 # Prefer Peter Claver
			OR = {
				culture = tuskegean
				culture = motowner
				culture = gullah
				culture = creole
				culture_group = caribbanglo
				culture_group = antillais
				culture_group = laurentian
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1031
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Knights of Columbus
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1031
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1031
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1032
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1032
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1033
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Knights of Columbus
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1032
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege refuses request to join the Knights of Columbus
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1033
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1050
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = neognostic
			religion = sedevacantist
			religion = nestorian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
				NOT = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = custom_usa
				region = world_central_canada
				region = world_western_canada
				region = world_central_america_caribbean
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_knights_of_columbus = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_knights_of_columbus = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_knights_of_columbus = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = custom_usa
					region = world_central_canada
					region = world_western_canada
					region = world_central_america_caribbean
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1051
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1051
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_knights_of_columbus = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1052
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1052
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1053
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1053
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1053
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.1054 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_columbus
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling a Christian Holy Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1060
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_liege_or_above = FROM
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1061
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when expelling a Christian Holy Order
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1061
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1061
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_EXPEL_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifier = donated_to_holy_order
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1061
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Knights of St John
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1130
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = neognostic
			religion = sedevacantist
			religion = nestorian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_knights_of_peter_claver
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = catholic
				religion = neognostic
				religion = sedevacantist
				religion = nestorian
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_peter_claver }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_peter_claver
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1131
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Knights of Peter Claver
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1131
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1131
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1132
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1132
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1133
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Knights of Peter Claver

	id = SoAtE.1132

	is_triggered_only = yes

			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target

					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to Peter Claver (also used for Men in Black and Columbus)
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1140
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = christian }
			FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1141
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { religion_group = oldworld }
			FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = CM.4399
				}
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

		}

			has_alternate_start_parameter = {

			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1150
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = neognostic
			religion = sedevacantist
			religion = nestorian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_knights_of_peter_claver = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = world_caribbean
				region = world_south_america
			}
		}
				
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_peter_claver }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_of_peter_claver
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_knights_of_peter_claver = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_knights_of_peter_claver = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_knights_of_peter_claver = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_knights_of_peter_claver = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = world_caribbean
					region = world_south_america
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1151
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1151
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_knights_of_peter_claver = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1152
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# The Grand Master demands one of your sons due to debt
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1200
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = atomicist
			religion = aphite
		}
		is_heretic = no
		has_character_modifier = borrowed_from_bektashi
		NOT = { has_character_flag = sent_son_to_bektashi }
		any_child = {
			is_female = no
			is_adult = yes
			is_ruler = no
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { 
					current_heir = { 
						character = PREVPREV 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				is_adult = yes
				is_ruler = no
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { 
						current_heir = { 
							character = PREVPREV 
						}
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1201
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1201
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_oppenheimer = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1202
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1202
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1203
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1203
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1203
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DEMAND_SON_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1003 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		set_character_flag = sent_son_to_bektashi
		
		piety = 100
		
		d_bektashi = {
			holder_scope = {
				FROMFROM = {
					move_character = PREV
					hidden_tooltip = {
						clear_wealth = PREV
					}
					end_inaccessibility_effect = yes #removes in_hiding or in_seclusion
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1003 # Pay them back
		wealth = -300
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_bektashi
		}
		FROM = {
			wealth = 300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_SOA_1003 # Refuse
		piety = -1000
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Oppenheimer Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1230
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = atomicist
			religion = aphite
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_oppenheimer
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = atomicist
				religion = aphite
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		liege = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = d_oppenheimer }
			liege = {
				NOT = { has_landed_title = d_oppenheimer }
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_oppenheimer }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_oppenheimer
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}

# The Grand Master requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1250
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		is_heretic = no
		OR = {
			religion = atomicist
			religion = aphite
		}

		d_oppenheimer = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
				NOT = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			port = yes
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_oppenheimer }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_oppenheimer
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_oppenheimer = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_oppenheimer = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_oppenheimer = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				port = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1251
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = SoAtE.1251

# The daughter of a ruler volunteers to join the St Ursula
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1330
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_women = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = ursuline
			religion = angeline
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_st_ursulas_chosen
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = ursuline
				religion = angeline
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_st_ursulas_chosen }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_st_ursulas_chosen
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			OR = {
				is_landed = yes
				is_pregnant = yes #Simply won't join if pregnant
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2

				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}

# The Grand Master demands one of your sons due to debt
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1400
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = americanist
			religion = hamiltonian
			religion = jeffersonian
			religion = libertarian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		has_character_modifier = borrowed_from_assassins
		NOT = { has_character_flag = sent_son_to_assassins }
		any_child = {
			is_female = no
			is_adult = yes
			is_ruler = no
			prisoner = no
			NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { 
					current_heir = { 
						character = PREVPREV 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_men_in_black }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_men_in_black
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
				is_adult = yes
				is_ruler = no
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { is_incapable = yes }
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { 
						current_heir = { 
							character = PREVPREV 
						}
					}
				}
			}
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1401
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1401
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_men_in_black = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1402
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1402
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1403
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1403
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1203
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DEMAND_SON_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1403 # Agree
		
		set_character_flag = sent_son_to_assassins
		
		piety = 100
		
		d_men_in_black = {
			holder_scope = {
				FROMFROM = {
					move_character = PREV
					hidden_tooltip = {
						clear_wealth = PREV
						add_trait = disinherited
					}
					end_inaccessibility_effect = yes #removes in_hiding or in_seclusion
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1003 # Pay them back
		wealth = -300
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_assassins
		}
		FROM = {
			wealth = 300
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { wealth = 300 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_SOA_1003 # Refuse

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Mystics" } }
			piety = -1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Mystics" }
			piety = -200
			set_character_flag = assassins_refused_to_pay_debt
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { wealth = 300 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_impious_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_dlc = "Mystics" }
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1423
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1223
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_assassins
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.1424 }
			}
		}
		
		piety = 100

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1003 # Pay them back
		wealth = -300
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_character_modifier = borrowed_from_assassins
		}
		FROM = {
			wealth = 300
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { wealth = 300 }
			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC_SOA_1003 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Mystics" } }
			piety = -1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "Mystics" }
			piety = -200
			set_character_flag = assassins_refused_to_pay_debt
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { wealth = 300 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_impious_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_dlc = "Mystics" }
			}
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Men in Black
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1430
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = americanist
			religion = hamiltonian
			religion = jeffersonian
			religion = libertarian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_men_in_black
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = americanist
				religion = hamiltonian
				religion = jeffersonian
				religion = libertarian
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_men_in_black }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_men_in_black
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1431
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1450
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = americanist
			religion = hamiltonian
			religion = jeffersonian
			religion = libertarian
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_men_in_black = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
				NOT = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			port = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_men_in_black }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_men_in_black
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240

			factor = 0.5

					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}

		}

			factor = 0.5

				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_men_in_black = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

				has_empty_holding = yes

# Ping event when expelling a Muslim Holy Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1460
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_liege_or_above = FROM
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1461
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling a Pagan Holy Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1560
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_liege_or_above = FROM
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1561
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when expelling a Pagan Holy Order
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1561
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1561
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_EXPEL_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		remove_character_modifier = donated_to_holy_order
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1061
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Brotherhood
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1630
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = evangelical
			religion = antinomian
			religion = charismatic
			religion = postadventist
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_national_cathedral
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = evangelical
				religion = antinomian
				religion = charismatic
				religion = postadventist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
				
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_national_cathedral }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_national_cathedral
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1631
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Brotherhood
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1631
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1631
	picture = GFX_evt_western_knights_byzantine
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1632
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1632
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1633
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Brotherhood
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1632
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_national_cathedral = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1650
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = evangelical
			religion = antinomian
			religion = charismatic
			religion = postadventist
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_national_cathedral = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_national_cathedral }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_national_cathedral
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_national_cathedral = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_national_cathedral = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_national_cathedral = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_national_cathedral = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1651
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1651
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_national_cathedral = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1652
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1652
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1653
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1653
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1653
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_national_cathedral
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.1654 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_national_cathedral
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1730
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = anabaptist
			religion = batenburger
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_lebanon_brethren
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = anabaptist
				religion = batenburger
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lebanon_brethren }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lebanon_brethren
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
						father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1731
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1731
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1731
	picture = GFX_evt_western_knights_byzantine
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1732
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1732
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1733
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1732
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_lebanon_brethren = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege refuses request to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1733
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1740
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1741
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the Order
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1741
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1141
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1750
	hide_window = yes

	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = anabaptist
			religion = batenburger
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_lebanon_brethren = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lebanon_brethren }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lebanon_brethren
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_lebanon_brethren = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_lebanon_brethren = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_lebanon_brethren = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_lebanon_brethren = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1751
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1751
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_lebanon_brethren = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1752
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1752
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1753
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1753
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1053
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lebanon_brethren
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.1754 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_lebanon_brethren
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Castle has been erected
province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1754
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1754
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1760
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1761
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when expelling the Order
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1761
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1061
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_EXPEL_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1061
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Judah Lions
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1830
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = rastafarian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_judah_lions
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion_group = afro_syncretic
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_judah_lions }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_judah_lions
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1831
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1851
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_judah_lions = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.1852
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1852
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1853
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1853
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1853
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_judah_lions
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.1854 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_judah_lions
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Castle has been erected
province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1854
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1854
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling the Judah Lions
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1860
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1861
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when expelling the Judah Lions
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1861
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1861
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_EXPEL_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1061
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Shomrim
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1930
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = jewish_group
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_shomrim
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion_group = jewish_group
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_shomrim }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_shomrim
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1931
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Shomrim
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1931
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_1931
	picture = GFX_evt_melee
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1932
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1932
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1933
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Shomrim
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1932
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_shomrim = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege refuses request to join the Shomrim
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1933
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

	id = SoAtE.1940
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1941
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
	}
}

					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {

				value = random

		}

	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion

		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.1950
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = jewish_group
	
	trigger = {
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_shomrim = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_shomrim }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_shomrim
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_zealots = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_shomrim = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_shomrim = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_shomrim = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.1951
			}
		}
	}
}

		d_shomrim = {

					id = SoAtE.1952
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Lords of the Sky
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2030
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = occultist_reformed
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_fm
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = occultist_reformed
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fm }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fm
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2031
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to the Lords of the Sky
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2040
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2041
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the Lords of the Sky
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2041
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_2041
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2050
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion = occultist_reformed
	
	trigger = {
		d_fm = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fm }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fm
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_fm = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_fm = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_fm = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_fm = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2051
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2051
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_fm = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.2052
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2052
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2053
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2053
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_2053
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fm
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.2054 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_fm
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Castle has been erected
province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2054
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_2054
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling the Lords of the Sky
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2060
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2061
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Flaming Sword
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2130
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = revelationist_reformed
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_flaming_sword
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = revelationist_reformed
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_flaming_sword }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_flaming_sword
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2131
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Flaming Sword
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2131
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_2131
	picture = GFX_evt_melee
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2132
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_2132
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2133
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Flaming Sword
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2132
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_flaming_sword = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the UAW
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2230
	hide_window = yes

	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = rust_cultist
			religion = chrome_cultist
		}
		is_heretic = no
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_uaw
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = rust_cultist
				religion = chrome_cultist
			}
			is_heretic = no
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
				
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_uaw }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_uaw
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2231
			}
		}
	}
}

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree

			factor = 100
		}

			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2232

			}
		}

		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse

				religion = FROM
			}

		}
		
		FROM = {

			}
		}
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2250
	hide_window = yes

	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = rust_cultist
			religion = chrome_cultist
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_uaw = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = custom_great_lakes
				region = world_northeast
			}
		}
		
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_uaw }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_uaw
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_uaw = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_uaw = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_uaw = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_uaw = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = custom_great_lakes
					region = world_northeast
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2251
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2251
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_uaw = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.2252
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = {

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_uaw
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.2254 }
			}

		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {

			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling the UAW
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2260
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2261
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Greenpeace
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2330
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = no
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = gaian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_keepers_of_the_green_peace
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = gaian
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_greenpeace }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_greenpeace
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
						father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2331
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_greenpeace
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.2354 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_greenpeace
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling the Greenpeace
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2360
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2361
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}
