# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Nauvoo Legion
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2430
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = latter_day_saints
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_nauvoo_legion
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			AND = {
				religion_group = latter_day_saints
				is_heretic = no
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_nauvoo_legion }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_nauvoo_legion
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2431
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Nauvoo Legion
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2431
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_2431
	picture = GFX_evt_throne_room_norse_pagan
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2432
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_2432
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2433
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Nauvoo Legion

	id = SoAtE.2432
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

				save_event_target_as = order_target

					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2450
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = latter_day_saints
	
	trigger = {
		is_heretic = no
		d_nauvoo_legion = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_nauvoo_legion }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_nauvoo_legion
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_nauvoo_legion = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_nauvoo_legion = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_nauvoo_legion = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_nauvoo_legion = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2451
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2550
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion = thelemic_reformed
	
	trigger = {
		d_oto = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_oto }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_oto
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_oto = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_oto = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_oto = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_oto = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2551
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2551
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_oto = {
			holder_scope = {

					id = SoAtE.2552
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2630
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = sacred_heart
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_masked_knights
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = sacred_heart
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_masked_knights }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_masked_knights
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
#		modifier = {
#			factor = 3.0 # Prefer the Order of Santiago
#			OR = {
#				culture_group = iberian
#				culture = andalusian_arabic
#			}
#		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2631
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Order

	id = SoAtE.2631
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_2631
	picture = GFX_evt_knight_kneeling
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2632
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_2632
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2633
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2730
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = falling_star
			religion = moravian
			religion = wormwoodist
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_order_of_brotherhood
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = falling_star
				religion = moravian
				religion = wormwoodist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_brotherhood }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_brotherhood
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
						father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
#		modifier = {
#			factor = 3.0 # Prefer the Order of Calatrava
#			OR = {
#				culture_group = iberian
#				culture = andalusian_arabic
#			}
#		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2731
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2731
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_2731
	picture = GFX_evt_knight_kneeling
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2732
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_2732
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2733
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2732
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		
		d_order_of_brotherhood = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege refuses request to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2733
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2740
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2741
			}
		}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the Order
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2741
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1141
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2750
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = falling_star
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_order_of_brotherhood = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = custom_neoladino
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_brotherhood }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_brotherhood
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_order_of_brotherhood = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_order_of_brotherhood = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_order_of_brotherhood = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_order_of_brotherhood = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2751
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2751
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_order_of_brotherhood = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.2752
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2752
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2753
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2753
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1053
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_brotherhood
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.2754 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_brotherhood
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153 # Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Castle has been erected
province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2754
	desc = EVTDESC_SOA_2754
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when expelling the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2760
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2761
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when expelling the Order
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2761
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOA_1061
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_EXPEL_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1061
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the Order
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2830
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		OR = {
			religion = high_church
			religion = nonconformist
		}
		is_heretic = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_st_pats
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			OR = {
				religion = high_church
				religion = nonconformist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_st_pats }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_st_pats
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}

			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}

			}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {

				id = SoAtE.2831
			}
		}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2850
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = high_church
			religion = nonconformist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_st_pats = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = world_eastern_canada
				region = world_central_canada
				region = world_northeast
				region = world_norselands
				region = world_rustlands
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_st_pats }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_st_pats
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_st_pats = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_st_pats = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_st_pats = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_st_pats = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.2851
			}
		}
	}
}

# Character joining holy order effects
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.2864
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_minor_title = title_commander
			}
			remove_title = title_commander
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_minor_title = title_appointed_regent
			}
			remove_title = title_appointed_regent
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_minor_title = title_patrician_heir
			}
			remove_title = title_patrician_heir
		}
		clear_wealth = event_target:order_target
		spouse = {
			remove_spouse = spouse
			character_event = { id = SoAtE.2863 }
		}
		move_character = event_target:order_target
		add_trait = celibate
		end_inaccessibility_effect = yes #removes in_hiding or in_seclusion
	}
}

########################################
# d_lightbringers
########################################

# Ping event when vassalizing the d_lightbringers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3000
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_defacto_liege = FROM
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3001
			}
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_lightbringers
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3001
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3001
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_lightbringers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3003
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = sol_invicta
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_lightbringers
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = sol_invicta
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lightbringers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lightbringers
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3004
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_lightbringers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3004
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3004
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3005
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_3004
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3006
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_lightbringers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3005
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_lightbringers = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege refuses request to join the d_lightbringers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3006
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to d_lightbringers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3007
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3008
				}
			}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the Hospitallers
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3008
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_3008
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3009
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion = sol_invicta
	
	trigger = {
		d_lightbringers = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = custom_empire_mexico
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lightbringers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lightbringers
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_lightbringers = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_lightbringers = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_lightbringers = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_lightbringers = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = custom_empire_mexico
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3010
			}
		}
	}
}

					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_lightbringers
			}
		}

			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.3013 }

		wealth = 100

# Ping event when expelling the new holy orders
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3060
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		any_title_under = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				location = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							character = FROM
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
						}
					}
				}
			}
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3061
			}
		}
		
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_expelled_from_realm
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_dead_sun
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3103
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = mictlantec
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_dead_sun
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = mictlantec
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_dead_sun }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_dead_sun
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3104
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_lightbringers

		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = custom_california
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_bears }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_bears
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_golden_bears = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_golden_bears = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_golden_bears = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_golden_bears = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = custom_california
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3210
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_bears
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.3213 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_bears
		}

		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {

		}

# Ping event when vassalizing the d_followers_arjuna

			letter_event = {

			}
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_followers_arjuna
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3301
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3301
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_followers_arjuna
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3303
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = hindu
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_followers_arjuna
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = hindu
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_followers_arjuna }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_followers_arjuna
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3304
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_golden_bears
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3304
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3304
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3305
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_3304
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3306
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_followers_arjuna

				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3411
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = SoAtE.3411
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3412
			}

	id = SoAtE.3412
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_3412
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_batallon_colombia
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.3413 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_batallon_colombia
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Ping event when vassalizing the d_saint_expedit
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3500
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_defacto_liege = FROM
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3501
			}
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_saint_expedit
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3501
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3501
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_saint_expedit
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3503
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = voodoo
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_saint_expedit
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = voodoo
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_saint_expedit }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_saint_expedit
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3504
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_saint_expedit
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3504
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3504
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3505
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_3504
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3506
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_saint_expedit
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3505
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_saint_expedit = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

	id = SoAtE.3507
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3508
				}
			}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3509
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion = voodoo
	
	trigger = {
		d_saint_expedit = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = world_caribbean
				region = world_gulf_coast
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_saint_expedit }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_saint_expedit
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_saint_expedit = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_saint_expedit = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_saint_expedit = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_saint_expedit = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = world_caribbean
					region = world_gulf_coast
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3510
			}
		}
	}
}

		d_saint_expedit = {

				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3511
				}
			}
		}
	}

# Ping event when vassalizing the d_warriors_guaicaipuro
character_event = {

			}

}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_warriors_guaicaipuro
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3701
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3701
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_warriors_guaicaipuro
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3703
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = espiritista
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_warriors_guaicaipuro
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = espiritista
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_warriors_guaicaipuro }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_warriors_guaicaipuro
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3704
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_warriors_guaicaipuro
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3704
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3704
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3705
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_3704
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3706
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_warriors_guaicaipuro
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3705
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to d_warriors_guaicaipuro
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3707
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3708
				}
			}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the d_warriors_guaicaipuro
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3708
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_3708
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3709
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion = espiritista
	
	trigger = {
		d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = world_south_america
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_warriors_guaicaipuro }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_warriors_guaicaipuro
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_south_america
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3710
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3710
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_warriors_guaicaipuro = {

				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3711
				}
			}
		}
	}

	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = candomble
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_capoeiristas
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = candomble
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_capoeiristas }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_capoeiristas
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3904
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_capoeiristas
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3904
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_3904
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3905
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_3904
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3906
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_capoeiristas
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3905
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_capoeiristas = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to d_capoeiristas
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3907
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3908
				}
			}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the d_capoeiristas
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3908
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_3908
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3909
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion = candomble
	
	trigger = {
		d_capoeiristas = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = world_south_america
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_capoeiristas }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_capoeiristas
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_capoeiristas = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_capoeiristas = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_capoeiristas = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_capoeiristas = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_south_america
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3910
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3910
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_capoeiristas = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.3911
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3911
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.3912
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.3912
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_3912
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_capoeiristas
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.3913 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_capoeiristas
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}

		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4003
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = brethren
	
	trigger = {
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_code_keepers
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = brethren
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_code_keepers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_code_keepers
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4004
			}
		}
	}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_golden_archers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4103
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = consumerist
			religion = monetarist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_golden_archers
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = consumerist
				religion = monetarist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_archers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_archers
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4104
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4109
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = consumerist
			religion = monetarist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_golden_archers = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = custom_usa
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_archers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_archers
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_golden_archers = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_golden_archers = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_golden_archers = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_golden_archers = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = custom_usa
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4110
			}
		}
	}
}

				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_golden_archers
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.4113 }

		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_round_table
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4203
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = pagan_group
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = celtic_pagan
			religion = celtic_pagan_reformed
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_round_table
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = celtic_pagan
				religion = celtic_pagan_reformed
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_round_table }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_round_table
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4204
			}
		}
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4309
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = evangelical
			religion = charismatic
			religion = antinomian
			religion = postadventist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_salvation_army = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = custom_greater_southeast_usa
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_salvation_army }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_salvation_army
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_salvation_army = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_salvation_army = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_salvation_army = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_salvation_army = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = custom_greater_southeast_usa
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4310
			}
		}
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_three_fires
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4403
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = american_native
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = midewiwin_reformed
			religion = midewiwin
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_three_fires
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = midewiwin_reformed
				religion = midewiwin
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_three_fires }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_three_fires
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4404
			}
		}
	}
}

				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4506
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4509
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = american_native
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = raven_tales
			religion = raven_tales_reformed
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_taxet_warriors = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = world_western_canada
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_taxet_warriors }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_taxet_warriors
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_taxet_warriors = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_taxet_warriors = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_taxet_warriors = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_taxet_warriors = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_western_canada
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4510
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4510
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_taxet_warriors = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.4511
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4512

		}
	}
}

	id = SoAtE.4512
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_4512
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_taxet_warriors
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.4513 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_taxet_warriors
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_fruit_of_islam
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4603
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = muslim
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = orientalist
			religion = misrist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_fruit_of_islam
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = orientalist
				religion = misrist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fruit_of_islam }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_fruit_of_islam
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4604
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_fruit_of_islam

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4709
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = muslim
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = traditionalist
			religion = revivalist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
		
		d_guardians_of_tradition = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = world_northeast
				region = custom_great_lakes
				region = world_south_america
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_guardians_of_tradition }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_guardians_of_tradition
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_guardians_of_tradition = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_guardians_of_tradition = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_guardians_of_tradition = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_guardians_of_tradition = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = world_northeast
					region = custom_great_lakes
					region = world_south_america
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4710
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4710
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_guardians_of_tradition = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.4711
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4711
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4712
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4712
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_4712
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_guardians_of_tradition
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.4713 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_guardians_of_tradition
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_coureurs_des_bois
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4801
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_4801
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_coureurs_des_bois
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4803
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = exovedate
	
	trigger = {		
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_coureurs_des_bois
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			religion = exovedate
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_coureurs_des_bois }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_coureurs_des_bois
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4804
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_coureurs_des_bois
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4804
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_4804
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4805
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_4804
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4806
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian

			religion = angeline
		}

				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}

		NOT = {

			}
		}

					is_landed = yes
				}

						father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child

		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {

		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {

		}
		modifier = {

				always = yes

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4909
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = ursuline
			religion = angeline
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
	
		d_knights_st_flanelle = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = world_central_canada
				region = custom_great_lakes
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_st_flanelle }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_st_flanelle
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_knights_st_flanelle = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_knights_st_flanelle = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_knights_st_flanelle = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_knights_st_flanelle = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = world_central_canada
					region = custom_great_lakes
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4910
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4910
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_knights_st_flanelle = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.4911
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4911
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.4912
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.4912
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_4912
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_st_flanelle
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.4913 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_knights_st_flanelle
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}
