# Notification event when vassalizing the d_cedesi
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5001
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5001
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_cedesi
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5003
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion = aphite
	
	trigger = {	
		is_heretic = no
	
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_cedesi
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			religion = aphite
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_cedesi }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_cedesi
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5004
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_cedesi
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5004
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5004
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5005
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_5004
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5006
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_cedesi

	id = SoAtE.5005
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

		d_cedesi = {

					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = world_great_plains
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_pony_express }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_pony_express
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_pony_express = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_pony_express = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_pony_express = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_pony_express = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_great_plains
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5110
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

		}
	}

		}

			}
		}

			FROMFROM = {

		wealth = 100

			}
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_order_of_the_golden_bunny
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5201
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5201
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_order_of_the_golden_bunny
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5203
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			religion = apostolic
			religion = celeste
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
	
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_order_of_the_golden_bunny
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = apostolic
				religion = celeste
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_the_golden_bunny }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_the_golden_bunny
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5204
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_order_of_the_golden_bunny
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5204
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5204
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5205
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_5204
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5206
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}

	}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5209
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = christian
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = apostolic
			religion = celeste
		}

		is_heretic = no
	
		d_order_of_the_golden_bunny = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = world_south_america
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_the_golden_bunny }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_order_of_the_golden_bunny
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_order_of_the_golden_bunny = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_order_of_the_golden_bunny = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_order_of_the_golden_bunny = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_order_of_the_golden_bunny = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_south_america
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5210
			}
		}
	}

			d_twelve_pairs_of_france = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_twelve_pairs_of_france = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_twelve_pairs_of_france = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_south_america
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5310
			}
		}
	}
}

			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_twelve_pairs_of_france
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.5313 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_twelve_pairs_of_france
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_legion_infernal
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5401

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_legion_infernal
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5403
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = pagan_group
	
	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			religion = aria_de_machete_reformed
			religion = aria_de_machete
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
	
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_legion_infernal
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = aria_de_machete_reformed
				religion = aria_de_machete
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_legion_infernal }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_legion_infernal
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5404
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_legion_infernal
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5404
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5404
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5405
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_5404
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5406
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5409
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"

	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = pagan_group
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = aria_de_machete_reformed
			religion = aria_de_machete
		}
	
		is_heretic = no
	
		d_legion_infernal = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			region = world_south_america
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_legion_infernal }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_legion_infernal
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_legion_infernal = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_legion_infernal = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_legion_infernal = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_legion_infernal = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				region = world_south_america
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5410
			}
		}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5510
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_iatse = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.5511
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5511
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5512
			}
		}
	}
}

letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5512
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_5512
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_BUILD_CASTLE_FOR_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1023
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_iatse
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROMFROM = {
				province_event = { id = SoAtE.5513 }
			}
			remove_character_modifier = expelled_d_iatse
		}
		
		piety = 200
		wealth = 100
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1153
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		
		piety = -100
	}
}

# Castle has been erected
province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5513
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5513
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			wealth = -300
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1024
		build_holding = {
		   type = castle
		   holder = FROMFROM
		}
	}
}

########################################
# d_iron_workers
########################################

# Ping event when vassalizing the d_iron_workers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5600
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_defacto_liege = FROM
		FROM = {
			letter_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5601
			}
		}
	}
}

# Notification event when vassalizing the d_iron_workers
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5601
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5601
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_iron_workers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5603
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			religion = rust_cultist
			religion = chrome_cultist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
	
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_iatse
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = rust_cultist
				religion = chrome_cultist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_iron_workers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_iron_workers
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5604
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_iron_workers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5604
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5604
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5605
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_5604
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5606
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_iron_workers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5605
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_iron_workers = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Liege refuses request to join the d_iron_workers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5606
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_refused_request_holy_order
		}
	}
}

# Ping event when donating money to d_iron_workers
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5607
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.5608
				}
			}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# Notification event when donating money to the d_iron_workers
letter_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5608
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC_SOATE_5608
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_alternate_start_parameter = {
					key = religion_names
					value = random
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = HOLY_ORDER_DONATE_MONEY_ALT
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	border = GFX_event_letter_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5609
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = rust_cultist
			religion = chrome_cultist
		}
	
		is_heretic = no
	
		d_iron_workers = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = custom_great_lakes
				region = world_northeast
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_iron_workers }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_iron_workers
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_iron_workers = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_iron_workers = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_iron_workers = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_iron_workers = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = custom_great_lakes
					region = world_northeast
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5610
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5610
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_iron_workers = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.5611
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {

# The son of a ruler volunteers to join the d_afl
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5903
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	only_men = yes
	min_age = 16
	max_age = 45
	only_capable = yes
	prisoner = no
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {	
		OR = {
			religion = rust_cultist
			religion = chrome_cultist
		}
		
		is_heretic = no
	
		is_ruler = no
		
		martial = 5
		
		is_title_active = d_afl
		
		OR = {
			father_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
			mother_even_if_dead = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
			}
		}
		
		liege = {
			holy_order = no
			is_heretic = no
			OR = {
				religion = rust_cultist
				religion = chrome_cultist
			}
			liege = {
				holy_order = no
				is_heretic = no
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_afl }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_afl
			}
		}

		NOT = {
			any_spouse = {
				OR = {
					is_landed = yes
					AND = {
						is_pregnant = yes
					father_of_unborn = { character = ROOT } # Won't happen if spouse is pregnant with non-bastard child
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			trait = zealous
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = celibate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = homosexual
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			trait = content
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = chaste
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { age = 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = slothful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = lustful
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = cynical
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = hedonist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = ambitious
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			any_heir_title = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			is_primary_heir = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_spouse = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 100 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		liege = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5804
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother asks to join the d_afl
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5804
	desc = EVTDESC_SOATE_5804
	picture = GFX_evt_crusaders
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA_SOA_1031 # Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = 100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5805
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOATE_5804
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB_SOA_1031 # Refuse
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = FROM
			}
			piety = -100
		}
		
		FROM = {
			character_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5806
				tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP_SOA_1033
			}
		}
	}
}

# Son or brother joins the d_afl

	id = SoAtE.5805
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_afl = {
			holder_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = order_target
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = SoAtE.2864 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

	id = SoAtE.5807
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		wealth = 300
		FROM = {
				letter_event = {
					id = SoAtE.5808
				}
			}
		opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = opinion_generous_donation
		}
		abdicate_holy_order_if_religion_changes_effect = yes
	}
}

# The Grand Master humbly requests the right to build a castle in your demesne
character_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5809
	hide_window = yes
	
	has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"
	min_age = 16
	only_playable = yes
	religion_group = oldworld
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = rust_cultist
			religion = chrome_cultist
		}
	
		is_heretic = no
	
		d_afl = {
			holder_scope = {
				wealth = 300
				NOT = {
					realm_size = 10
				}
			}
		}
		
		any_demesne_province = {
			has_empty_holding = yes
			OR = {
				region = custom_great_lakes
				region = world_northeast
			}
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_afl }
		NOT = {
			any_liege = {
				has_character_modifier = expelled_d_afl
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_afl = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			d_afl = {
				holder_scope = {
					NOT = { demesne_size = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_afl = {
				holder_scope = {
					num_of_count_titles = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			d_afl = {
				holder_scope = {
					realm_size = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_demesne_province = {
			limit = {
				has_empty_holding = yes
				OR = {
					region = custom_great_lakes
					region = world_northeast
				}
			}
			province_event = {
				id = SoAtE.5810
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = {
	id = SoAtE.5810
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		d_afl = {
			holder_scope = {
				character_event = {
					id = SoAtE.5811
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
